		install  -m 644 /tmp/opensipsctl.mysql \
			/tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/lib/opensips/opensipsctl/opensipsctl.mysql ; \
		rm -fr /tmp/opensipsctl.mysql ; \
		sed -e "s#/usr/local/share/opensips#/usr/share/opensips/#g" \

		touch           /tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/lib/opensips/opensipsctl/opensipsdbctl.mysql ; \

		for FILE in scripts/mysql/drouting-create.sql scripts/mysql/b2b_sca-create.sql scripts/mysql/avpops-create.sql scripts/mysql/acc-create.sql scripts/mysql/dialplan-create.sql scripts/mysql/call_center-create.sql scripts/mysql/domainpolicy-create.sql scripts/mysql/cachedb_sql-create.sql scripts/mysql/siptrace-create.sql scripts/mysql/fraud_detection-create.sql scripts/mysql/domain-create.sql scripts/mysql/speeddial-create.sql scripts/mysql/group-create.sql scripts/mysql/registrar-create.sql scripts/mysql/standard-create.sql scripts/mysql/usrloc-create.sql scripts/mysql/load_balancer-create.sql scripts/mysql/imc-create.sql scripts/mysql/permissions-create.sql scripts/mysql/cpl-create.sql scripts/mysql/rls-create.sql scripts/mysql/dispatcher-create.sql scripts/mysql/alias_db-create.sql scripts/mysql/presence-create.sql scripts/mysql/uri_db-create.sql scripts/mysql/dialog-create.sql scripts/mysql/b2b-create.sql scripts/mysql/registrant-create.sql scripts/mysql/msilo-create.sql scripts/mysql/rtpproxy-create.sql scripts/mysql/pdt-create.sql scripts/mysql/carrierroute-create.sql scripts/mysql/userblacklist-create.sql scripts/mysql/closeddial-create.sql scripts/mysql/auth_db-create.sql ; do \

		mkdir -p /tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/lib/opensips/opensipsctl ; \

		touch           /tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/lib/opensips/opensipsctl/opensipsdbctl.pgsql ; \
		install  -m 644 /tmp/opensipsdbctl.pgsql /tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/lib/opensips/opensipsctl/ ; \
		rm -fr /tmp/opensipsdbctl.pgsql ; \
		mkdir -p /tmp/opensips/pkg/opensips/usr/share/opensips//postgres ; \
		for FILE in scripts/postgres/drouting-create.sql scripts/postgres/b2b_sca-create.sql scripts/postgres/avpops-create.sql scripts/postgres/acc-create.sql scripts/postgres/dialplan-create.sql scripts/postgres/call_center-create.sql scripts/postgres/domainpolicy-create.sql scripts/postgres/cachedb_sql-create.sql scripts/postgres/siptrace-create.sql scripts/postgres/fraud_detection-create.sql scripts/postgres/domain-create.sql scripts/postgres/speeddial-create.sql scripts/postgres/group-create.sql scripts/postgres/registrar-create.sql scripts/postgres/standard-create.sql scripts/postgres/usrloc-create.sql scripts/postgres/load_balancer-create.sql scripts/postgres/imc-create.sql scripts/postgres/permissions-create.sql scripts/postgres/cpl-create.sql scripts/postgres/rls-create.sql scripts/postgres/dispatcher-create.sql scripts/postgres/alias_db-create.sql scripts/postgres/presence-create.sql scripts/postgres/uri_db-create.sql scripts/postgres/dialog-create.sql scripts/postgres/b2b-create.sql scripts/postgres/registrant-create.sql scripts/postgres/msilo-create.sql scripts/postgres/rtpproxy-create.sql scripts/postgres/pdt-create.sql scripts/postgres/carrierroute-create.sql scripts/postgres/userblacklist-create.sql scripts/postgres/closeddial-create.sql scripts/postgres/auth_db-create.sql ; do \
